		<category name="Borderlands 2 Item Ports">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>By Aaron0000</comment>
				<comment>Converts many items in the Pre-Sequel into items from Borderlands 2 (with BL2 Community Patch Buffs applied when applicable). You'll need to pick and activate the ones you want, they are all off by default.</comment>

				<comment>NOTES;</comment>
				<comment>Several of these items aren't true 1-to-1 copies of their Borderlands 2 counterpart. They're as close as I can feasibly get in Pre-Sequel.</comment>
				<comment>Some of these weapons take the "firing mode" from other weapons in order to actually function. If they do, they'll be labeled something like "XXXX Replacer (Uses XXXX Firing Mode). Some of them even alter the original weapon they took the firing mode from to make them work properly again and have a "Fix" folder of some sort in them. usually in the Stats folder.</comment>
				<comment>Some of these items change what parts can normally spawn or not spawn on them. If you run a game without this mod active, the items in question will disappear.</comment>
				<comment>Credit to Laxlife for the Twister, I mostly just added the skin to it.</comment>
			</category>
